	writefile_22();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/ClassLoader.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/ClassLoader.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/ClassLoader.php') != 'd4a058aaad78183c3f2e53b04c63beb617c3f6db') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/ClassLoader.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/ClassLoader.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/ClassLoader.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/ClassLoader.php') !== 'd4a058aaad78183c3f2e53b04c63beb617c3f6db') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/ClassLoader.php') !== '8d9f47db4e033e631ebc6dc1f0bd282d23bdaa97') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/ClassLoader.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/ClassLoader.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/ClassLoader.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/ClassLoader.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_22();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/ClassLoader.php') !== 'd4a058aaad78183c3f2e53b04c63beb617c3f6db') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/ClassLoader.php');

		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/autoload_static.php') !== '405ab39e189537fc1a5f5afef0bf4e6820729702') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/autoload_static.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/autoload_static.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/autoload_static.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/autoload_static.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_28();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/autoload_static.php') !== '750b01bca67da63de616da75a269e1b2ef71bc98') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/autoload_static.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.json');
	writefile_29();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') != 'fc1c1bcd3642dfef16092fe680f7a672b1c8f912') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'fc1c1bcd3642dfef16092fe680f7a672b1c8f912') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'f0243d2e7277836c5d01809029d9789dcd6a20ba') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_29();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'fc1c1bcd3642dfef16092fe680f7a672b1c8f912') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.php');
	writefile_30();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') != 'ed8f98e1d0dedf23a1d8f2f66ae118c9a9a653de') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== 'ed8f98e1d0dedf23a1d8f2f66ae118c9a9a653de') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== 'b26696ab3a57b9b80f9e1f4d2070632f811b7407') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_30();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== 'ed8f98e1d0dedf23a1d8f2f66ae118c9a9a653de') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/src/sha3.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/emn178/js-sha3/src/sha3.js');
	writefile_37();
	if (!is_file('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/src/sha3.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/emn178/js-sha3/src/sha3.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/src/sha3.js') != 'f54089da5a0766574c84a2d4fa42b37562b37318') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/emn178/js-sha3/src/sha3.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/src/sha3.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/emn178/js-sha3/src/sha3.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/src/sha3.js') !== 'f54089da5a0766574c84a2d4fa42b37562b37318') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/src/sha3.js') !== '857c8f4a1cba456999e84ecfe24bb3e1e5491d7a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/emn178/js-sha3/src/sha3.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/src/sha3.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/src/sha3.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/src/sha3.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_37();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/emn178/js-sha3/src/sha3.js') !== 'f54089da5a0766574c84a2d4fa42b37562b37318') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/emn178/js-sha3/src/sha3.js');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/licenses')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/licenses');
	writefile_38();
	if (!is_file('vendor/licenses')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/licenses');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/licenses') != '00c30dc383e8ce6783b516ff93c232cb7a7c0e00') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/licenses');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/licenses', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/licenses');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== '00c30dc383e8ce6783b516ff93c232cb7a7c0e00') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== '121f76dd266ed2ad86c58a1631bac00380f0df2e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/licenses');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/licenses');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/licenses')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/licenses', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_38();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/licenses') !== '00c30dc383e8ce6783b516ff93c232cb7a7c0e00') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/licenses');
		}
	}
}
